  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f6d1b480-0723-4e45-8fe7-adb307c01e66'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer4545033552482859244">The ruthless Empress Amara of Kraeshia has taken the Mytican throne, and now uncertainty looms over the three kingdoms. Since Lucia unleashed the fire Kindred, wreaking havoc throughout the land, Myticans have been looking for someone—anyone—they can trust. They believe in Amara, not knowing her grand promises are built on lies.<br/><br/>In Paelsia, Magnus and Cleo reluctantly follo</span>
  <span id="freeText4545033552482859244" style="display:none">The ruthless Empress Amara of Kraeshia has taken the Mytican throne, and now uncertainty looms over the three kingdoms. Since Lucia unleashed the fire Kindred, wreaking havoc throughout the land, Myticans have been looking for someone—anyone—they can trust. They believe in Amara, not knowing her grand promises are built on lies.<br /><br />In Paelsia, Magnus and Cleo reluctantly follow King Gaius to the home of his exiled mother, Selia. Selia is a powerful witch and claims she can help unlock the magic of the Kindred—<i>if</i> the visitors agree to her terms. When Jonas arrives from Kraeshia, he is shocked to find that his rebel army now includes his sworn enemies. Along with Nic, Felix, and the mysteriously resurrected Ashur, the contentious group agrees to cast aside old grudges—for now—and united against their common enemy: Amara.<br /><br />Meanwhile, bearing the child of a Watcher and feared by all, Princess Lucia travels across Mytica to find her family. But time is running out. The impending storm signals the dark prophecy Timotheus warned her about. Her fate is written, and it includes none other than the rebel Jonas. When their paths collied, Jonas and Lucia must decide between blindly following their destiny or fighting for their own free will.<br /><br />The battle for power culminates at the Paelsian palace, where Amara resides. Rain pours. Blood spills. And soon all will discover that the darkest magic comes at an even darker price.</span>

    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1170312358?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1170312358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6755200303788667605"><b>Well, I definitely need some liquid help to deal with <i>this</i> ending.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381001438ra/3761882.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When the storm comes, all will be revealed.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23367261.Crystal_Storm__Falling_Kingdoms___5_' title='Crystal Storm (Falling Kingdoms, #5) by Morgan Rhodes' rel='nofollow noopener'>Crystal Storm</a> is indeed a storm. <b>A storm of confusion, anger, vengeance, magic, love and greed.</b> Power is a devious thing. It can corrupt the purest soul, cloud the sharpest mind, make everything seem pale compared to the knowledge, the intoxicating feeling that you can bend anything and anyone to your will. And that's what the Kindred, what the elemental deities offer. But </span>
  <span id="freeText6755200303788667605" style="display:none"><b>Well, I definitely need some liquid help to deal with <i>this</i> ending.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381001438ra/3761882.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When the storm comes, all will be revealed.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23367261.Crystal_Storm__Falling_Kingdoms___5_" title="Crystal Storm (Falling Kingdoms, #5) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Crystal Storm</a> is indeed a storm. <b>A storm of confusion, anger, vengeance, magic, love and greed.</b> Power is a devious thing. It can corrupt the purest soul, cloud the sharpest mind, make everything seem pale compared to the knowledge, the intoxicating feeling that you can bend anything and anyone to your will. And that's what the Kindred, what the elemental deities offer. But this power always comes with a price. The land of Mytica is in the brink of destruction. The new empress is ruthless, and the forces that can stop her don't trust each other in order to work together. Loyalties are tested. Convictions are shaken. And a sorceress, a rebel, a golden princess and a dark prince are caught in the eye of this storm.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Power is all that matters, Magnus. Legacy is all that matters.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>It is no secret that the Falling Kingdoms series <b>holds a special place in my heart</b>. I am always able to lose myself in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5295120.Morgan_Rhodes" title="Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Morgan Rhodes</a>'s epic tale, a tale infused with legends, gods and mortals, intrigue and power games. Her ingredients? <b>Deception, manipulation and secrets</b> and you question even your most beloved characters. <b>Deaths and resurrections</b> and your jaw drops to the floor. <b>Magic</b>, raw magic and your fingers tingle with the anticipation, the need to unleash it and wreck havoc. <b>Greed</b> and <b>love</b> in an eternal and lethal dance. And <b>morally grey characters</b>.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I think we all deserve to die for something we've done. Or for something we've failed to do.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Where I come from, when something impossible happens we say that <i>"a bakery must have been demolished"</i> (don't ask me why, we're weird people). Well, in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23367261.Crystal_Storm__Falling_Kingdoms___5_" title="Crystal Storm (Falling Kingdoms, #5) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Crystal Storm</a>'s case I think that every single bakery in Mytica mush have been demolished, because I never expected the day would come when <i>Jonas Agallon</i> would be the most sensible and levelheaded character. But it's true. He was reasonable, and tried hard to not let the bitterness he harbored and his pain guide him and lead him to dark paths. Can't say the same for Lucia though, who was still a psycho bitch, but she did try to make amends for the mayhem she created and the innocent blood in her hands, so <i>maybe</i> she can return to the decent human being she was once upon a time.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“True leaders often must be ruthless enough to steal and murder. If they don't, someone else will.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And that's Magnus, <b>my precious cinnamon roll</b>. His philosophy is still the same,<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1481827949ra/21459826.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>he's dark and moody and prone to violence, but his complexity, the battle between light and darkness he keeps fighting, are some of the many reasons I love him so much. And so does Cleo. They have some wonderful scenes together, but unfortunately it was Cleo that prevented me from giving <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23367261.Crystal_Storm__Falling_Kingdoms___5_" title="Crystal Storm (Falling Kingdoms, #5) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Crystal Storm</a> the fifth star.<br>She's been my favorite heroine since book 1. Yet, I found her really spiteful and greedy, sometimes acting like the spoiled child she once was, and all these horrible things she said to Magnus, and her constant desire to hide her feelings for him because she was ashamed really disappointed me. Of course Magnus is not an easy-going, charming fellow, but he needs someone to believe in him, and Cleo's faith sometimes wavered. I still ship them though. <b>Hard.</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Love is pain. Love is death. And love strips one of their power.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And since I love all these flawed characters, you can imagine how I'm going to spend the months until the final book's release.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1481827949ra/21459827.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/katerina_papas/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/KaterinaPapas" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/Booknest.eu/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="http://booknest.eu/index.php/component/k2/item/288-crystalstorm" rel="nofollow noopener">BookNest</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6755200303788667605" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Or let the gifs say it for me !! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484691235ra/21742580.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484691235ra/21742581.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I couldn't figure out whether to go with a 4 or a 5 star review so I kept it at 4. <br><br>Things that happened in this book! **NO SPOILERS**<br><br>Sooooooo, that ending. <div id="review_1473732651" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1473732651" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1473732651?book_show_action=true">Dec 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=witches">witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1473732651" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5182595629228590750">1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1455382903' rel='nofollow noopener'>Falling Kingdoms</a> ★★★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1470781684?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rebel Spring</a> ★★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1471808405?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Gathering Darkness</a> ★★★★★<br/>4.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1466480405?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Frozen Tides</a> ★★★★★<br/><br/>Out of all the feelings I expected to have while reading <i>Crystal Storm</i> I never thought disappointment would be one of them, or the most prominent. <i>Crystal Storm</i> was, hands down, no question, my most anticipated book of 2016. It was even on my rough draft list of "best books published in 2016" because I was so confident it would be perfection incarnate. Oh, how wrong I was.<br/><br/>Instead of perfection, we got p</span>
  <span id="freeText5182595629228590750" style="display:none">1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1455382903" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Kingdoms</a> ★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1470781684?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Rebel Spring</a> ★★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1471808405?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Gathering Darkness</a> ★★★★★<br>4.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1466480405?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Frozen Tides</a> ★★★★★<br><br>Out of all the feelings I expected to have while reading <i>Crystal Storm</i> I never thought disappointment would be one of them, or the most prominent. <i>Crystal Storm</i> was, hands down, no question, my most anticipated book of 2016. It was even on my rough draft list of "best books published in 2016" because I was so confident it would be perfection incarnate. Oh, how wrong I was.<br><br>Instead of perfection, we got plot holes, unnecessary angst between Cleo and Magnus, a cliffhanger ending that felt like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1385323421" rel="nofollow noopener">Empire of Storms</a> part two, and twists that I feel bad even calling twists because they came out of nowhere and were so unexpectedly bad. I'm so let down that I'm actually at a loss for words.<br><br>And what makes it worse is that this book has Magnus on the cover. How can anything with a picture of Magnus Damora be less than perfection? I mean, I know 2016 was a bad year for most of us, but this... this I never saw coming.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1481856385ra/21462026.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyways, this is the fifth book in the <i>Falling Kingdoms</i> series that, until this point, have only gotten better and better. This series follows four young adults and their different inner struggles for power, vengeance, and love. We also have some side characters along for the ride. A lot of people compare this series to a young-adult <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/976868255" rel="nofollow noopener">Game of Thrones</a>, and I think that description is pretty accurate. <br><br>One of those four main characters, Magnus is one of my favorite characters ever written. His internal struggle, but the way the others perceive him from his outward actions, is one of the best things I've ever read in my life. He is, and always will be, my little cinnamon roll that is far too good for this world.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I want you,” he whispered against her lips. “I want you so much I may die from it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Seriously, all I want for Christmas is Magnus Damora. Please, Lord, help me with this unhealthy thirst for a fictional character. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1481856385ra/21462027.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The only person, besides the perfect Magnus, that I even overly enjoyed was Amara. Like, I understand she was sort of the villain, even though now her dynamic is quite shifted (oh please, Felix, give me the <i>good</i> angst.) My favorite types of villains are the villains that make sense, and Amara, to me, makes perfect sense. She comes from a long line of female oppression, and she is finally able to pave her own path. Seeing the continued abuse by her own subjects, just because of her gender, made for a really good read, and she really wormed her way into my heart. I have nothing but high hopes for her (and Felix) for the final installment.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It is never too early for girls to learn to speak their minds. It’s a habit that will make them braver and stronger as they grow up.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Surprisingly, Lucia's POV was pretty enjoyable, too. I even shed a few tears while a certain prophecy was being told and acted out. Jonas was also amazing, and I loved how he stepped up. Also, he always knows what to say. Both of these characters really stood out among all of the forced twists and plot devices. <br><br>I actually hated a lot of characters in this book: I hated Nic; he's such a little weasel. I hated Taran; talk about <i>more</i> unnecessary angst. I borderline hated Ashur, just because of his action at the end with Cleo. I still hate Gaius, because nothing has changed even though the story wants you to believe it has. And I obviously hated the out of the blue villain that Morgan Rhodes decided to sloppily write in. <br><br>Elena, Cleo's deceased mother, is obviously a key to much more that we don't realize yet. Cleo is most likely going to turn out to be even more of a special snowflake from the events that took place at the end of this book. But as long as she doesn't keep starting stupid, pointless drama, and keep pushing the paragon that is Magnus away, I won't hate her. <br><br>I mean, even with all the disappointments this book had, I'm still too invested to stop right before <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1840492666" rel="nofollow noopener">the final installment</a>, but I for sure won't have as high of hopes as I did for <i>Crystal Storm</i>, and it won't be making any of my anticipation lists.<br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany/profile" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="5182595629228590750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1417971810" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1417971810" />
    <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee"><img alt="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583262285p2/44137919.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1417971810?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee">Mikee (ReadWithMikee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1417971810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5741961966817218555"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481773617i/21453766._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>***No spoilers. Just major, incoherent fangirling. I apologize in advance.***</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>OKAY. WTF WAS THAT ENDING??? I swear to god, Morgan Rhodes will be the death of us all.</b><br/><br/>First off, I just wanted to say that going into Crystal Storm, I didn't think it would even come close to being my favorite book in this series. I actually found the first 150 pages to be painfully slow and pointless to the point where I was ready to dock off a star for the pacing alone. BUT once we did surpass 150 pages, SHIT WEN</span>
  <span id="freeText5741961966817218555" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481773617i/21453766._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>***No spoilers. Just major, incoherent fangirling. I apologize in advance.***</i>
</b><br><br><b>OKAY. WTF WAS THAT ENDING??? I swear to god, Morgan Rhodes will be the death of us all.</b><br><br>First off, I just wanted to say that going into Crystal Storm, I didn't think it would even come close to being my favorite book in this series. I actually found the first 150 pages to be painfully slow and pointless to the point where I was ready to dock off a star for the pacing alone. BUT once we did surpass 150 pages, SHIT WENT DOWN. I couldn't put the book down at all. I thought Crystal Storm would suffer from the "middle book syndrome" or "the book before the finale syndrome" but boy have I never been so wrong in my life! Morgan Rhodes does not know how disappoint. Although she does know how to make you hate her and love her at the same time. So there's that.<br><br>If you know me and my obsession with the Falling Kingdoms, you would know that I live for Magneo. So let me just say that no matter how many cute and steamy moments we get between Magnus and Cleo, IT WILL NEVER BE ENOUGH. I seriously just need a book with just Magneo from beginning to end. I don't care about anything else or anybody else. Like, what's a Lucia? I can seriously forget about everyone else in the book and just immerse myself in everything Magneo. It hurts. It really hurts to be a Magneo shipper. My love for them knows no bounds.<br><br>Okay, let me be serious for one second because I can't be fangirling like this throughout my whole review. XD No more mentions of Magneo after this. Promise.<br><br>I thought this book wouldn't even come close to topping Frozen Tides but now that I finished this book and had some time to think about it, Crystal Storm just might be my new favorite book in the series. I surprise even myself. Just seeing how short this book was compared to the other books in the series, I was so sure that I would be in for the biggest disappointment ever, but nope. Not even close. That one year of waiting was worth the wait and now we're back to the waiting game once again. :'(<br><br>Also, this book was annoying. I loved it. But definitely the most annoying book I've ever read lol. The characters are all infuriating. Except for Magnus because he is the epitome of perfection. No one is worthy of him. Well, except for Cleo but let me hold myself back before I start fangirling about Magneo again.<br><br>Anyways, infuriating. All these peasants. Lucia, as always. Amara might actually be even more annoying than Lucia. Jonas was actually useful in this book. Nic was and always has been irrelevant to me. Ashur was ???. Felix was a precious cinnamon roll that I didn't expect to steal the show with his witty, hilarious lines. Cleo was great as always except for the last 50 pages (like girl, what were you even thinking?). Magnus was perfection. OMG. That reminds me.<br><br>MAGNUS. MY POOR BABY. I'm sorry you have to endure your... predicament for a whole year but we're with you every step of the way suffering as much as you until next December.<br><br>I don't know how Morgan Rhodes does it but the Falling Kingdoms series never fails to improve with each book. Not a lot of authors can pull off a six-book series but holy crap does Morgan have us wrapped around her finger. Just when you think she can't surprise you anymore, she pulls all this shit and leaves you with all these feelings for a year. We're all going to be in for such a treat for the finale. I bet Morgan Rhodes is just chilling and plotting our demise and ways she can rip our hearts out in the final book because that ending though...<br><br>DYING. I'm dying, I tell you! I can't even write a proper review right now with all these feelings. Bye.</span>

<div id="review_1669420388" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1669420388" />
    <a title="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink"><img alt="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568991289p2/50044222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1669420388?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink" href="/user/show/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink">Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=chelsea-bones">chelsea-bones</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=best-anti-heroes">best-anti-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink?shelf=recommended-fantasy">recommended-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1669420388" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12161889374279073361">Good gracious. EoS and now this? Bloody hell. 2017 better bring us some happiness. <br/><br/>Alright. There will be some spoilers up to book 4 in here and I'll try to be vague about the rest.<br/><br/>If it has been a while since you read the first four books- I recommend doing a skim at least of the last book. There are seriously so many characters and I had a little trouble getting back in to the world. This picks right back up on the cliffhanger in book 4 and there are some small recaps but honestly I forgot who</span>
  <span id="freeText12161889374279073361" style="display:none">Good gracious. EoS and now this? Bloody hell. 2017 better bring us some happiness. <br><br>Alright. There will be some spoilers up to book 4 in here and I'll try to be vague about the rest.<br><br>If it has been a while since you read the first four books- I recommend doing a skim at least of the last book. There are seriously so many characters and I had a little trouble getting back in to the world. This picks right back up on the cliffhanger in book 4 and there are some small recaps but honestly I forgot who I even cared about. <br><br>Lie. Really I only care about Magnus and Cleo. I'm pretty sure most of the fandom agrees. If those are the characters you are attached to- I think you'll like this book. I remember not caring in the slightest about any of the other characters and was in agony though any POV that wasn't either of them in other books. This book actually felt a bit more bearable because Mags and Cleo darling seem to be the focus in this one (thank goodness) so even the other POVs revolve around them for the most part. (More on them later...)<br><br>I'm actually happy to report that Lucia was mildly tolerable in this book too. She is feeling a little remorseful for what all went down before, and it was *semi* interesting to try and figure out what path she will choose now. Don't get me wrong- I still can't stand her. Jonas actually was kinda useful in this one *gasp* and I was kinda interested in him finally. My least favorite bits were Amara's POV. Blah blah, I get it... you hate men... you want to rule everything... yada yada. <br><br>Everyone else seemed to be tools to move along the story but the book was so short it didn't drag too much. On that note - no one is safe, yet again. Plenty of death if you're here for that kinda thing.<br><br>Back to more important matters...<br><br>I absolutely loved the direction the author went for Magnus and Cleo- though it thoroughly wrenched my heart. Just because they "got together" in the fourth book and confessed their love DOES NOT MEAN things are smooth rolling for them. Magnus is still so very wounded from his past and Cleo faces some difficulties that make them doubt each other. They very obviously love each other but the relationship struggles in this were so painful. But you know what? That makes the good moments so worth while... and there are some GOOD moments. Not to mention- they still have some heated banter which YES I LOVE IT UGH. The best part which I applaud Rhodes for is THEY DID NOT ONCE GET CHEESY like so many couples after they get together. <br><br>THAT ENDING WHAAAAAAAT WAS THAT. Okay but I'm hopeful because that just can't be it. That's all I can say without being emotional. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465306084ra/19338476.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My only complaint aside from some of the boring POVs throughout the series is the writing. Maybe it is just me- but I feel like Rhodes tries too hard with some of her dialogue. So much of it just feels unatural/cheesy. The writing isn't the strongest either but whatever- Magnus and Cleo make up for any series shortcomings. It also tends to be a little under descriptive at times which confused me - especially during some of the high action scenes towards the end. <br><br>Lastly, yep... playlist for Magnus (and some Cleo feels..) because I can't not do it. Check it out <a href="https://open.spotify.com/user/brilia/playlist/3r0vbSHPNyVIrE4ANjBfBW" rel="nofollow noopener">Here!</a> if you want to give it a listen! <br><br><a href="http://www.herbookishthings.com" rel="nofollow noopener">My Blog</a> ~ <a href="https://www.instagram.com/reverieandink/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ~ <a href="https://twitter.com/reverieandink" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ~ <a href="https://www.etsy.com/shop/reverieandink" rel="nofollow noopener">Etsy</a></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1669443989" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1669443989?book_show_action=true">Nov 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1669443989" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11944544936590643421"><br/><b>RELEASED TODAY EVERYONE GO BUY MY MAGNUS BABY!!!!!! And for those friends who are getting ready to embark on this wonderful journey (*cough* Brittney, Pea *Cough*)-SPAM ME. 'kay bye.</b><br/><br/>I feel like its so far and few between that I get a chance to write a (well thought out) review for a book I love. For example, I’ve been sick off and on for five months, and <b>my reading has been basically non-existent</b>…but in the last couple months, I’ve managed to read some of my favorite books this year-and maybe 3 </span>
  <span id="freeText11944544936590643421" style="display:none"><br><b>RELEASED TODAY EVERYONE GO BUY MY MAGNUS BABY!!!!!! And for those friends who are getting ready to embark on this wonderful journey (*cough* Brittney, Pea *Cough*)-SPAM ME. 'kay bye.</b><br><br>I feel like its so far and few between that I get a chance to write a (well thought out) review for a book I love. For example, I’ve been sick off and on for five months, and <b>my reading has been basically non-existent</b>…but in the last couple months, I’ve managed to read some of my favorite books this year-and maybe 3 of them have gotten even close to the reviews I’m capable of and that they deserve. So, when I received the email telling me I got one of my most (ummm come on, basically THE book that I pined for most) anticipated reads of this year…I just knew I would give it the best review I could muster.<br><br>So, this is me taking the opportunity to talk about one of my top book boyfriends this year-Magnus. And doesn’t he deserve the whole review to himself, honestly?? I mean seriously…he’s Magnus, the prince of blood. Do I really need to say anything more?<br><br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_n892fdZJlE1sicas5o1_500_zps3hbohvxy.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480709065ra/21342190.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n892fdZJlE1sicas5o1_500_zps3hbohvxy.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Well, I think I do, for those who want to know about more than my darling boy. And let’s be honest-Everyone who reads this series is obsessed with him, and some might only be reading it because of him, so what more can I possibly push?<br><br>Basically, even after all the trials and tribulations surrounding all the books before…<b>this one broke my heart the most</b>. It was absolutely the most brutal. I’ll admit that it isn’t near as brutal in the way of battle and death and destruction, but <b>more brutal in matters of the heart</b>. My soul was ripped to shreds in more ways than one, and more times than one. I might be a bit of a drama queen, but my heart has always ripped in two when a couple like Cleo and Magnus, so in love, have to keep themselves a secret with literally everyone around them. <br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_n1n4y6fwQQ1tt6rtko1_500_zpsoga8wzsa.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480709065ra/21342188.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n1n4y6fwQQ1tt6rtko1_500_zpsoga8wzsa.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was definitely a tremulous chapter for the new couple, bringing heartaches and new issues bubbling to the surface. But <b>not once did my confidence in them waver</b>. Not once did I think one or the other would cheat (even with easy access) or give up on their new love. And not once did I think they wouldn’t believe in the best of each other, in the end, keeping their relationship stronger than ever. But I <i>did</i> foresee some bumps in the road...and that prediction aimed true.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “And you listen to <i>me</i>, Princess.” Gaius’s voice followed her like a rancid odor. “This love you think you feel for my son? The day will come when you will have to choose between Magnus and power. And I know, without a doubt, that you will choose power.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_inline_n9phx0SQq91qcp4l4_zpsiz69jyic.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480709065ra/21342189.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_n9phx0SQq91qcp4l4_zpsiz69jyic.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So many book series these days drag out unnecessarily for so many books you can’t help but roll your eyes at them-but there are some that <b>shine brighter with each book</b>, building into something so tangible that you can’t breathe when it’s left unfinished. You aren’t thinking, <i>‘Oh, come on, another book?!’</i>, you’re rejoicing that there’s another and you have the opportunity to follow the paths <br>these relationships and evil plots continue to pave. <b>This is one of those series</b>.<br><br>Even as I worried there were going to be too many books when I started this series, I remain surprised each and every time I open a Falling Kingdoms book. <b>They grow dramatically richer and more complex with each additional storyline</b>, and you can’t help but to love each character, good or bad, more with each new installment. <br><br>For example, had I only stayed on book one, I only would have lightly pined for Magnus. Sure, he was the reason I even <i>considered</i> continuing onward with the story, but I put this series down for a couple months after finishing, if only because there was so much more to read in my TBR pile and nothing had truly hooked me, aside from the not-so-sweet man candy. But, the minute I was urged to continue on, <b>I was immediately hooked</b>. <br><br>The deep love, the betrayals upon betrayals, the needless slaughters…they spoke to my evil self in a way I’ve not been accustomed to, in a while. This series (and especially these last three stories) touched on so many nerves that I couldn’t help but to be hooked. Now, months later, <b>I’m a ravenous fangirl who can never have enough Magnus and Cleo</b>. <br><br>I think it’s safe to say who my two favorite characters are, hmm? But even as the series has progressed, I find I have many favorites, especially in this one-Even the evil Amara. There’s just something about an extra feisty bitch added to the character pool that enriches the story and adds just the right amount of turmoil. <br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/tumblr_n6daprMPUK1rawb5do1_500_zpsytetscck.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480709065ra/21342191.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n6daprMPUK1rawb5do1_500_zpsytetscck.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And, truthfully, this book wasn’t as action packed as the rest, the more I think about it. In all truth, I think that’s why I loved this book so much and it became my absolute favorite of the 5. <b>We really got time to sit and see where everyone stood</b>, who was loyal and who wasn’t, what relationships were real and which were smoke and mirrors. I even found the guard relationships to be enriching to the story. By our main cohorts all staying in the same place for an extended amount of time, we really had the opportunity to see the chaos as it slowly descended upon them. <br><br>When a story is just go-go-go, you lose a little something, I think. But as Mags and Cleo sat in one particular area for a prolonged amount of time, surrounded by both friend and foe, <b>we got to see some relationship turmoil that ripped me apart</b>, but filled me with ceaseless obsession for the two. I don’t know why this book spoke to me the most (maybe because I’m messed up in the head and <b>love jealousy so much its sick</b>), but it did, and I already am dying to re-read it and the whole series. I might just do it!! WATCH AND SEE! <br><br>With a cliffhanger that took my breath away (and made me gleeful, yes I’m THAT crazy and THAT sick) I am already eagerly anticipating how it will all turn out in the final book. <b>Hearts will be broken</b>. Not everyone will survive. Loyalties and friendships will be tried and tested…and <b>I can’t help but long for the final book to be in my hands at this exact moment</b>. It hurts…but I guess I’ll just have to remember all the hot Magneo moments to get me through the next year. And, hey, I can always re –read this series multiple times as I wait. ;)<br><br><i>*Many thanks to the publisher for an advanced copy!*</i><br><br>For more of my reviews, please visit:<br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea-peril-please-reviews/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Hands down my favorite of the series.....I am so honored to have received this ARC!! Magpie-I LOVE YOU SO MUCH!!!!!!! <b>My heart is literally so broken...and I have so long to wait!!!</b><br><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/chelsea-peril-please-reviews/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1836559423" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1836559423" />
    <a title="Samantha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10067920-samantha"><img alt="Samantha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590018789p2/10067920.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1836559423?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha" href="/user/show/10067920-samantha">Samantha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1836559423" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15522808066344843014">This still felt like a Falling Kingdoms book so fans may not be as let down as I was. But this book felt very rushed and off balance. With the amount of characters, we didn't have enough time even with the core 4 to really see development from them. We had some character back tracking that felt unnecessary. Twists had no foreshadowing so they felt misplaced. And there were some tropes pulled out that I felt were ridiculous. It doesn't feel as consistent as the previous installments, which have c</span>
  <span id="freeText15522808066344843014" style="display:none">This still felt like a Falling Kingdoms book so fans may not be as let down as I was. But this book felt very rushed and off balance. With the amount of characters, we didn't have enough time even with the core 4 to really see development from them. We had some character back tracking that felt unnecessary. Twists had no foreshadowing so they felt misplaced. And there were some tropes pulled out that I felt were ridiculous. It doesn't feel as consistent as the previous installments, which have consistently gotten better and built upon one another. This feels separate in some way. <br /><br />I still enjoyed it! I love this world and these characters, and I'm always happy to see them. There were some developments and back stories that I loved seeing more of. But with how rushed this felt, it does make me nervous for the last book. <br /><br />Video review/discussion to come!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15522808066344843014" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1836559423">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1825844315?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zoha " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zoha " href="/user/show/48320485-zoha">Zoha </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48320485-zoha?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48320485-zoha?shelf=wtf-ending">wtf-ending</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1825844315" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16144345485642686741"><i>Buddy-read with Sara, here is her <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1839189206' rel='nofollow noopener'>review</a>, which, you'd want to read after my mindless ramble!</i> <br/><br/>Umm... where shall I start??? Alright, who I am kidding! I am sure as hell gonna start with my babies MAGNEO!! This book lived up to all my expectations and then some! Its a no brainer that I absolutely loved this book! <br/><br/><b>
  <u>And, oh! Spoilers ahead: Proceed with caution! :P</u>
</b><br/><br/><b>=>My favorite Prince and my beloved Princess are back,</b> feisty and sarcastic as they ever are, to face the <u>horror that is <i>Kraeshian Em</i></u></span>
  <span id="freeText16144345485642686741" style="display:none"><i>Buddy-read with Sara, here is her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1839189206" rel="nofollow noopener">review</a>, which, you'd want to read after my mindless ramble!</i> <br><br>Umm... where shall I start??? Alright, who I am kidding! I am sure as hell gonna start with my babies MAGNEO!! This book lived up to all my expectations and then some! Its a no brainer that I absolutely loved this book! <br><br><b>
  <u>And, oh! Spoilers ahead: Proceed with caution! :P</u>
</b><br><br><b>=&gt;My favorite Prince and my beloved Princess are back,</b> feisty and sarcastic as they ever are, to face the <u>horror that is <i>Kraeshian Empire &amp; Co.</i></u>!! But they faced them well at least for the first half of the book. :D Then shit hit the fan! And I was like this: <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479412794ra/21188129.gif" width="450" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>=&gt;My biggest concern after I read the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1825838927?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Frozen Tides</a> was</b> that now my OTP is canon they are gonna turn into love-sick puppies. <s>Don't blame me I read a lot of SJM this year!</s> But thanks to Morgan Rhodes, she managed to chisel just the right amount of romance balanced with adventure and plot twists. Although there new-found love almost doomed when Gaius told them about a certain curse, they have had their <i>cutesy moments! </i><br><br>=&gt;In case you forgot, this book covers a bunch of other characters as well; <b>lets talk about Gaius</b> first since the prologue was from his POV. Surprisingly, we saw a slightly different Gaius in this book.I always enjoyed Gaius's character. He is a great villain and I always say that villains decide how strong the plot is going to be. He has always planned something new for our MC but after the rather fatal fall that he survived, his behavior towards Magnus changed somewhat. I actually can't believe I cared for his well-being in the story but it was ultimately for the well-being of my favorite characters because he actually seemed to care about Magnus! Yeah, I know it is kinda difficult to grasp but it is true! <br><br><b>=&gt;There is an addition of Selia Damora amongst the Damoras.</b> Gaius's mother, an Oddling and even more cruel than her son if that is even possible but she is. A lot of things happened because of her but I don't want to talk about her a lot. <br><br><b>=&gt;Moving on to Jonas..., there is prophesy about him now???</b> Seriously? It seems only Magnus is the MC without any prophesies popping out of his head! That is sooooo unfair, Rhodes!! You are discriminatory towards my favorite Damora!! -_- Talking about Jonas and the prophesy about him, idk why but I found it bogus. So very bogus! Oh, and I forgot to mention <i>Timothious visited Jonas dreams.</i> I gotta say out of every immortal's visit in a mortal dream, Tim's visit in Jonas were the most entertaining; Jonas attitude toward Tim was hillarious. <br><br><b>=&gt;Lucia annoyed the hell outta me in previous books</b> and I can't say otherwise about her in this one. Although Lucia is on her path of redemption, she is still annoying. I also wanted her reunion with her family which didn't happen in this book. There are more prophesies about her that do not interest me one bit to be honest! <br> <br><b>=&gt;Amara is bitchy more than ever!</b> In previous books, we atleast got to see her vulnerable side, she had none in this one. I was expecting a rekindle of her romance with Felix but that also did not happen. Much to my disappointment, we saw a very little of Felix. <br><br><b>=&gt;THE ENDING!!!!</b>Lets not talk about the ending. It wrecked me. I don't want to remember I ever read that. NO. Absolutely not! I haven't read that guys! Not at all. Not yet! I don't know what happened in the last chapter. Don't try to remind me! -_- <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404450877ra/10239375.gif" width="500" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Now, excuse me while I gush over my OTP!</b>
</u><br><br><b>Cleo:</b> “How do you stand this temperature for so long?” she asked him.<br><b>Magnus:</b> “It must be my frozen heart.”<br><b>Cleo:</b> “Here I thought that had melted just a little around the edges.”<br><b>Magnus:</b> “Oh, no. All Limerians have frozen hearts. We <u>melt into puddles in places like Auranos.</u> ”<br><br><br>__________________________________________________________<br><br>I love this book and it is not even published yet! <i>That</i>, my friend, is some <u>true love!</u></span>

<div id="review_1800698791" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1800698791" />
    <a title="Caitlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/57334157-caitlin"><img alt="Caitlin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1507948675p2/57334157.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1800698791?book_show_action=true">Dec 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caitlin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caitlin" href="/user/show/57334157-caitlin">Caitlin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57334157-caitlin?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1800698791" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8067851367700813903"><i>Buddy read with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1674254787?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>May (who regrets giving me permission to start this book)</a><br/><br/><b><i>????? What....did.....i......just......read...... </i></b></i><br/><br/>I actually read this in 7 hours because I just sat down and read until it was over. I regret nothing at all because it was so fucking amazing. <br/><br/>This is, by far, my favourite in the <i>Falling Kingdoms</i> series. I have 0 clue how an author can fill that much action and that much drama into a 379 page book. It honestly has me at a loss of words. I was so sad going into this knowing </span>
  <span id="freeText8067851367700813903" style="display:none"><i>Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1674254787?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">May (who regrets giving me permission to start this book)</a><br><br><b><i>????? What....did.....i......just......read...... </i></b></i><br><br>I actually read this in 7 hours because I just sat down and read until it was over. I regret nothing at all because it was so fucking amazing. <br><br>This is, by far, my favourite in the <i>Falling Kingdoms</i> series. I have 0 clue how an author can fill that much action and that much drama into a 379 page book. It honestly has me at a loss of words. I was so sad going into this knowing that it's the shortest of the series so far but god dammit it did not disappoint me one bit. I actually started reading this series about 2 weeks ago and now I'm officially caught up and I have to wait with everyone else for the LAST BOOK. How on Earth is the next one going to be the last book?! I'm SO not ready to leave these amazing characters and fantastic world behind. <br><br><b>This review will be filled with low key spoilers but I promise to mark the big ones!</b><br><br><i>“There’s been so much that’s been sacrificed on this road we’ve travelled together. So much loss for both of us. But I hold tight to the thought that it will all be worth it in the end.”</i><br><br>Let's just talk about the characters for a minute because OMFG THERE WAS SUCH AMAZING CHARACTER DEVELOPMENT FOR A FEW CHARACTERS AND HONESTLY I'M JUST SO IN LOVE WITH THESE CHARACTERS - EVERY SINGLE ONE OF THEM.<br><br><b>Magnus</b> is my precious darling baby and I will defend him like my life depends on it. <br><br><i>"There would be no mercy here. But Magnus Damora would not beg for his own life."</i><br><br>In this one, he goes through a lot. He's only just really gotten together with Cleo when it's basically put on hold due to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the curse that turns out to not even be a curse - basically Cleo was supposed to die if she got pregnant so Magnus is like k I can't give her any affection anymore because I can't lose her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> His father also almost died but now he's alive due to dark magic and he grandmother is back and she's bat shit crazy. Also when the rest of the gang join Magnus and Cleo, he has to hide his love for her because everyone else basically hates Magnus. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The ending left Magnus in the worst state because he's LEGIT BEING BURIED ALIVE BY KURTIS THE BIG FAT PAIN IN THE ASS WHO I SAID NEEDED TO DIE LAST BOOK. Honestly that ending for Magnus was hell on Earth and I am hella stressed <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><i>“I know I can be horrible sometimes. I know it. But . . . I love you. That hasn’t changed.”<br>Her shoulders tensed. “Love isn’t enough to fix this.”</i><br><br>^^ ok this scene was so not okay man. Magneo is my life and the fact that Cleo said LOVE ISN'T ENOUGH TO FIX THIS to Magnus after they fought makes me crazy. I just need a happily ever after for them. I don't even care anymore.<br><br><b>Cleo</b> has always been a favourite character of mine and honestly she never disappoints me. She's so freaking strong and I swear the bombshells never stop when it comes to her. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[First she's dropped with the news of a curse and then she ends up getting water magic because the water kindred chose her.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>"I love him. I love Magnus with all my heart. And I swear, if he's ... dead ... if I've lost both Nic and Magnus today ..." Her voice broke as she raised her gaze, seeing that the others now watched her with fear in their eyes. The bottomless sensation of cool, powerful, water magic flowed just beneath the surface of her skin, as if waiting to be unleashed. "I don't think the world will survive my grief."</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>My love for <b>Lucia</b> has once again been restored. She went a bit crazy in <i>Frozen Tides</i> and ended up in a crazy situation but she's chilled out a bit now. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The fact that she's pregnant and the youngest of our cast still makes me stressed. Also she ended up having her entire pregnancy throughout this 1 book because it was fast tracked by her being at the sanctuary. Honestly, I would have loved it if she got the chance to meet up with Magnus and the King while she was pregnant just to be like SURPRISE!!!! But I guess we will get that when she rocks up with a baby. My heart broke when Lucia named her baby Lyssa after Lysandra. It was so sweet. And the fact that the prophecy said that Lucia will die and Jonas will raise the baby made me ridiculously stressed. As much as I was pissed at Lucia, I really do love her as character and I'd definitely miss her if she died. Also, the fact that Jonas had a prophecy saying he would look after Lucia's SON made me consider a lot. Lucia ended up having a daughter. Does that mean she's going to have ANOTHER baby and Jonas will look after that one? and "as if it were his own" then maybe it IS his own? Maybe Lucia and Jonas will have a baby but then she'll die in child birth?? Honestly I'm just trying to come up with any theory at the moment. <br><br><i>"Tell my brother, my father ... tell them that I'm sorry I hurt them. Tell them that I love them, and that I know they loved me. And tell ... tell my son when he's old enough to understand that there was good in me. Way deep down, anyway."</i>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Jonas</b> grew so much in this book. Honestly I wasn't his biggest fan in the past 4 books even though I still liked him as a character. After the events of <i>Frozen Tides</i> he's actually grown so much and become ridiculously wise. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He also has some idle magic now that he has both Olivia's and Phaedra's healing magic soaked into him. I'm still high key in shock about this. I have a note written down saying: "JONAS HAS MAGIC OMFG WHAT" and that pretty much sums up my feels. Also there's this new prophecy for him and I'm pretty sure Lucia and Jonas might end up being together and raising little Lyssa and I'm totally happy with it. I'm completely ready to start shipping this.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><i>"I belive in magic. In evil sorceresses who deep down are really beautiful princesses. I believe in immortals who live in a different world than this one, accessible by magical stone wheels. But you know what I don't believe in?"<br>"What?"<br>"I refuse to believe we have absolutely no control over our own futures, because right now? I'm damn well going to control my own."</i><br><br><b>Felix</b> is also someone I grew to love in this book. I think Jonas sums him up best by saying:<br><i>"That’s right. Former fearsome assassin for King Gaius. Currently fighting the good fight as he embarks on a long and arduous path to redemption. And also currently heaving his breakfast into the sea as an offering to any fish who may give assistance.”</i><br><br>As much as I hate <b>Amara</b> who is basically just a savage bitch, I get where she's coming from and I'm low key like YES BITCH GIRL POWER whenever she wants to take down a whole bunch of men. However, she's also really crazy and life would be so much easier if she just died.<br><br><b>King Gaius</b> (who I still find funny that he's named after a whole bunch of mad kings from history) actually had a teeny tiny bit of redemption. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[We learn that he was in love with Elena, Cleo's mother, and he took a potion to stop feeling things after his mother killed Elena. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> However, he's still annoying and we still need him dead because he's still after Cleo's head. <br><br><i>"Love is pain. Love is death. And love strips one of their power."</i><br><br><b>Nic</b> is someone who I expected to die in book 1 and yet here he still is. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[His ending makes me stressed because he's got Kyan inside of him. How do we get him out of there???????  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Ashur and Nic end up professing their love for each other (finally) and I actually really liked how it was so casual like oh yeah Nic likes boys too. <i>This is how it should be done - it should be casual rather than some big reveal.</i><br><br>Look, I'm never going to be able to fully explain what the hell the shit storm that was Crystal Storm. As I say in all my reviews for this series, if you haven't read this series already then you really <b>really</b> need to, okay?<br><br>Basically here's a sum up in gifs:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380437441ra/884558.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390260628ra/8178546.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1483176401ra/21585432.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436550302ra/15476172.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429882032ra/14639971.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1674254787" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12018443969858397338"><br/><i> It’s January 1st, my first read of 2017 and it’s ended in heartbreak, the future is not looking bright. </i><br/><br/>Its common courtesy to not give your <b> READERS A HEARTATTACK </b> while they’re reading. Thanks.<br/><br/><i> Crystal Storm </i> is the fifth book in the <i> Falling Kingdom’s </i> series and holds the award, by far, for the most beautiful cover. <br/><br/>I don’t think anyone is gonna argue with me on that. I mean just, look . . . <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464570259i/19252007._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> Crystal Storm, </i> in my humble opinion, is the best book from the series. Where the other books lacke</span>
  <span id="freeText12018443969858397338" style="display:none"><br><i> It’s January 1st, my first read of 2017 and it’s ended in heartbreak, the future is not looking bright. </i><br><br>Its common courtesy to not give your <b> READERS A HEARTATTACK </b> while they’re reading. Thanks.<br><br><i> Crystal Storm </i> is the fifth book in the <i> Falling Kingdom’s </i> series and holds the award, by far, for the most beautiful cover. <br><br>I don’t think anyone is gonna argue with me on that. I mean just, look . . . <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464570259i/19252007._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> Crystal Storm, </i> in my humble opinion, is the best book from the series. Where the other books lacked for plots and dramatic endings, <i> Crystal Storm </i> made up for it with lots of action, magic, and a heart shattering ending that just leaves you feeling like (ಥ﹏ಥ)<br><br>Still using the multiple point-of-views, I found this book to have the most seamless switch from them all. There wasn’t an abruptness with the change in point-of-views like the other books in the series, it was actually quite easy to devour (though it might be bc I’m 110% invested in this series now.)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483316947i/21600606._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I refuse to reveal much about the plot, <i> bc spoilers </i> but I will say that the character development and the friendships and allies and enemies that were made in this book made my head swirl. So much took place in 379 pages (I’m disappointed in the page count too, tbh, need more pages).<br><br>I must remark on #Mangeo because they are <b> everything </b> and we didn’t get nearly enough scenes of them. I didn’t read through 5 books only to have A COUPLE OF MANGEO SCENES. Get yourself together, Morgan Rhodes. <br><br>I. SIMPLY. NEED. MORE. MANGEO. AND. NOW.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483316947i/21600607._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, protect Mangus. That child needs to be protected at all costs, omg, my heart is still hurting from that ending.<br><br><br><i> "Love is pain. Love is death. And love strips one of their power." </i><br><br><br><br><b> 5 stars </b> for cruel, cliffhanger ending!!! :) :) :) :)<br><br><br>~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~ ~<br><br><br><br><i> My buddy read partner, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/57334157" rel="nofollow noopener">Cait the Chill-less Cloud</a> has ditched me by reading the whole book while I was asleep. <br><br></i></span>

<div id="review_1898034440" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1898034440" />
    <a title="Jiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana"><img alt="Jiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540380229p2/10502567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1898034440?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jiana" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana">Jiana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780448494166" href="/book/show/33371681-crystal-storm">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10502567-jiana?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1898034440" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer853927523602077854"><b>:) :) :) Hello Cliffhanger, my name is Jiana and you just put me in <b>hell</b>. Since I have to wait nine long months for the final book, I'll just pretend you never happened. Bye. :) :) :)</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491299602ra/22394341.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I'm writing this review and I have a killer headache. Why? Because I stayed up till 4 AM to binge this book, finish it, and cry over it. <br/><br/><u>Bad decision clearly.</u><br/><br/>I have come to realize this series makes me make bad decisions. Especially since I read every single book in less than a day. It's not my fault the series is </span>
  <span id="freeText853927523602077854" style="display:none"><b>:) :) :) Hello Cliffhanger, my name is Jiana and you just put me in <b>hell</b>. Since I have to wait nine long months for the final book, I'll just pretend you never happened. Bye. :) :) :)</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491299602ra/22394341.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I'm writing this review and I have a killer headache. Why? Because I stayed up till 4 AM to binge this book, finish it, and cry over it. <br><br><u>Bad decision clearly.</u><br><br>I have come to realize this series makes me make bad decisions. Especially since I read every single book in less than a day. It's not my fault the series is great and addictive, okay. I was supposed to be adult-ing but I decided to dedicate my day for Crystal Storm. Bad decision again. See? Bad decisions all around. Do I care though?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397738ra/767724.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Guys, listen. If you still haven't read this series, what are you waiting for? GO PICK UP FALLING KINGDOMS AND BLESS YOUR LIFE. But, warning: <u>there will be lots of pain.</u> Way, way, way more than joy, to be honest. <b>The series is 98% pain, 2% joy.</b> Morgan Rhodes likes to kill her readers just like she enjoys killing her characters. <u>However, the only confirmed death is my death.</u><br><br>Honestly, I just adore this series and I CAN'T BELIEVE THE DAMN CLIFFHANGER IT ENDED IN. I feel so numb. I can't believe I have to live <i>nine more months</i> with this pain. Can I get a time machine, please? I refuse this ending. I have decided to live in denial till Immortal Reign comes out. Excellent idea.<br><br>The book was so short. Honestly, I needed more. I always need more! Anyway, everything's gone to shit. No one is happy. No one is okay. Everything is just really bad. <br><br><b>I do need to mention something important: MAGNEO. Magneo is what I live for. I WILL GO DOWN WITH THIS SHIP, YOU GUYS.</b> They broke me 49288 times over the course of this series. But the greatest pain was in this book. <br><br>I adore the characters, you guys. <b><u>Magnus Damora</u> is my favorite. He is my precious baby and I will protect him at all times.</b> He suffers the most in this book and I. am. not. okay. with. this. one. bit. <u>Cleo</u> has developed immensely since book 1. She's so strong and brave now and I just adore her. She's definitely one of my all-time favorite heroines. <u>Lucia</u> is a character I hate but I also love. I wanted to punch her in GD and FT, but in CS, I just wanted to hug her and protect her, because LUCIA IS A SMOL BABY AND DOESN'T DESERVE BAD THINGS. <u>Jonas</u>, oh Jonas... I have a love/hate relationship with him. I hated him greatly in FT, but here in CS? He grew on me again and I found his development great. As for the side characters, <u>Felix</u> is my precious baby. <u>Amara</u> can die for all I care. I really like <u>Ashur</u> but I admit he stressed me out in this book. <u>Nic</u> is so annoying. I understand him and I get the reason behind everything he does. But he still annoys me. As for <u>King Gaius</u>, death to you.<br><br>It is so difficult to talk about these characters without going into spoilers, hence why I won't discuss the plot. So much has happened in a span of 379 pages and I don't know how Morgan Rhodes managed to do that. Frozen Tides remains my favorite between the books, but Crystal Storm was just as action-packed and perfect.<br><br><b>Friendly reminder: Read the books.</b><br><br>I just adore this series so much, you guys and thinking about it makes me cry.</span>
  <a data-text-id="853927523602077854" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
