<div id="review_2059002921" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2059002921" />
    <a title="Ahmed  Ejaz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53694260-ahmed-ejaz"><img alt="Ahmed  Ejaz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598778737p2/53694260.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2059002921?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ahmed  Ejaz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ahmed  Ejaz" href="/user/show/53694260-ahmed-ejaz">Ahmed  Ejaz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53694260-ahmed-ejaz?shelf=full-lengths">full-lengths</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53694260-ahmed-ejaz?shelf=2017">2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2059002921" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3200008824779679047"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Life isn’t guaranteed, not at any time, not for anyone. Every single day, every single moment, could be our last."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Woah!! This book was full of actions. I couldn't put it down. So far this book is the best in the series.<br/><b>
  <i>
    <u> This review is a pure spoiler. Read it at your own risk. </u>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><br/>=> So, Gaius doesn't die in this one as I was desperately hoping. I don't know what to feel about him now after THAT revelation. My hatred for him has dwindled a bit but not nullify yet. Perhaps in </span>
  <span id="freeText3200008824779679047" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Life isn’t guaranteed, not at any time, not for anyone. Every single day, every single moment, could be our last."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Woah!! This book was full of actions. I couldn't put it down. So far this book is the best in the series.<br /><b>
  <i>
    <u> This review is a pure spoiler. Read it at your own risk. </u>
  </i>
</b><br /><br /><br />=&gt; So, Gaius doesn't die in this one as I was desperately hoping. I don't know what to feel about him now after THAT revelation. My hatred for him has dwindled a bit but not nullify yet. Perhaps in the next book, it will.<br /><br />=&gt; Ashur came back from death! I should have guessed how far before him telling it because author had given the hint in the last book. Anyway, I don't think that he played out well in this book. He is just too optimistic. It's a good thing. But sometimes it can be deadly.<br /><br />=&gt; Taran. An unnecessary complication. I felt this way before. But after THAT ending, I think he wasn't that unnecessary. <br />He was a rebel and the fact that he just murdered only one person didn't pacify me. He forgave Magnus. Even though I wasn't completely satisfied by this, I was still happy. Because there was no more threat for Magnus from him.<br /><br />=&gt; Lucia. She did nothing important in this book except for giving birth to her daughter. I am curious that is her daughter a Watcher or a Sorcereres or both or just an ordinary mortal? Last option doesn't sound good to me. But anyway looking forward to it.<br /><br />=&gt; Now two Kindred are free. One of the amazing things happened in this book.<br /><br />=&gt; Water Kindred has become a part of Cleo! Amazing! It means she will be able to control it in the next book. Great!<br /><br />=&gt; Nic. Sometimes he becames a headache for me. I completely understand his reasons. But still sometimes it was difficult for me to handle him. I didn't feel a thing when he was dying. But the aftermath of it wasn't good for me to endure. Then I wished he shouldn't be dead. And thank God Lucia had saved him. <br />Now Fire Kindred has occupied his body. An interesting twist that whether Nic is still alive or not. Honestly, I really wish him dead. I am not seeing any further use of him anymore.<br /><br />=&gt; Jonas. He is the one I liked from beginning of the series. Now he has become a very important character for me in this series. I am happy that he has gained control over air elementia. It's amazing. <br />He and Lucia very much sound like Magnus and Cleo when they talk with each other. Well, No matter what! I still felt the absence of Lysandra here. <br /><br />=&gt; Gaius and Elena, Cleo's mother had a story! It was strange yet interesting.<br /><br />=&gt; NOW THE MAIN THING WHICH WILL BE KILLING ME TILL THE RELEASE OF THE LAST BOOK! <br />MAGNUS! What will happen to him?! After THAT ending, I can't stop thinking about it. For the answer, I have to wait for five months!! 😢😢😢😭😭😭<br /><br /><b>P.S: </b>The cover of this book is my favourite! I am soo obsessed with this that this cover has been my mobile's wallpaper even before I started this series. I won't lie. This is the only reason I started this series. :D<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I love Magnus with all my heart. And I swear, if he’s . . . dead . . . if I’ve lost both Nic and Magnus today . . .” Her voice broke as she raised her gaze, seeing that the others now watched her with fear in their eyes. The bottomless sensation of cool, powerful water magic flowed just beneath the surface of her skin, as if waiting to be unleashed. “I don’t think this world will survive my grief"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br /><br />July 15, 2017</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wren (fablesandwren)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wren (fablesandwren)" href="/user/show/42780417-wren-fablesandwren">Wren (fablesandwren)</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42780417-wren-fablesandwren?shelf=not-shelved">not-shelved</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1860901358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5969470616403406393">This series is going to drive me absolutely crazy. <br/><br/>Magnus and Cleo are an absolute joke. Like who knew this marriage that they were forced into was going to be even more complicated than an arranged marriage? And why does <b>every single male person ever</b> have a massive crush on Cleo? Like she is either “the most beautiful girl so-and-so has ever seen” or she is “a goddess walking among men”.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501977006ra/23515956.gif' alt='' width='350' height='195' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Like, I get it; she isn’t just an average looking girl. She’s a princess and she happens to be like really pr</span>
  <span id="freeText5969470616403406393" style="display:none">This series is going to drive me absolutely crazy. <br><br>Magnus and Cleo are an absolute joke. Like who knew this marriage that they were forced into was going to be even more complicated than an arranged marriage? And why does <b>every single male person ever</b> have a massive crush on Cleo? Like she is either “the most beautiful girl so-and-so has ever seen” or she is “a goddess walking among men”.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501977006ra/23515956.gif" alt="" width="350" height="195" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Like, I get it; she isn’t just an average looking girl. She’s a princess and she happens to be like really pretty. Just like the other princess (Lucia) who is equally a goddess walking among men but with dark hair instead of blonde. <b>Why can’t a princess ever just be average looking?!</b><br><br>Anyway, Magnus and Cleo are the ships of all ships. I love their relationship because it wasn’t like an “insta” thing, it was something that evolved. I mean, they legit hated each other (and sometimes I think they still hate each other). But that’s what makes it so intoxicating! <br><br>Amara is succeeding in her quest to take over all the kingdoms and be supreme leader of all the lands. <br><br>Jonas is somehow still alive.. literally have no idea why this guy is still alive.. like seriously does he have nine lives? Why are you a big player in this? I DON’T UNDERSTAND YOUR PURPOSE.<br><br>Lucia is pregnant with a baby growing inside of her at super speed. That in itself worries me. Like is this a demon that is just going to kill everyone? Because I feel that might be the only way this series can end.<br><br>Gaius is in the same state that he was at the end of the book; but, you start to see a different side of him besides just supreme evil-ruler overlord. Oh, and you meet his mother: that is a treat in itself.<br><br>Oh and the dead come back to life; because in the fantasy world, death isn’t permanent the majority of the time. Seriously, I think this is kind of a cheat; but, then again I am usually overjoyed to see a character come back to life. Bipolar feelings for a book is my usual though.<br><br>Oh and there’s something about the gods of the elements and someone trying to take back their world.<br><br>Honestly, this world-building has been phenomenal. It has been slow, but it doesn’t leave you confused about anything. The characters have grown a lot since the first book and they never seem to be acting out of their usual. You end up loving the characters for their flaws and stupidity and you morn them when they die (because a lot of people die. Literally the majority of the characters you meet die. Not a drill.). <br><br><u>
  <b>AND THAT ENDING</b>
</u> Like... WHY IS THE NEXT BOOK NOT IN MY HANDS? Cliffhangers are the ABSOLUTE WORSE. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501977006ra/23515957.gif" alt="" width="350" height="239" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everyone is NOT where they are suppose to be and there is NO happily ever after in this book and I need this to be fixed. <b>DO YOU HEAR ME RHODES? FIX THESE ENDINGS PLEASE!</b><br><br>---<br><br>Ummmm EXCUSE ME? Magnus is where and Cleo has what now? I NEED THE NEXT BOOK PLEASE</span>

  <span id="freeText5960733800044257894" style="display:none"><b>5 Golden Stars</b><br><br>98%<br><br>second favourite!<br><br><br>AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA! THE CLIFFHANGER! I must say I was waiting for something like this to happen (more like Wanting or even Needing! more thrills, the better! yep, Evil me!) since book 3 &amp; now it happened in the worst possible way &amp; blew me down off the CLIFFHANGER!<br>It chills my blood even by merely remembering it!<br>I love that feeling! you know? it made me feel alive! *mad laughter*<br>The ending including the Cliffhanger itself worth 5 stars Complete!!! but there's more to this book, so yep, 98%!<br>but I'm so glad that I can put my hands on book 6 at the moment! it feels kind of like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2169298809" rel="nofollow noopener">Goblet of Fire</a> ending!<br><br>enough of the ENDING way of the book &amp; more into the whole book:<br><br>*clearing my throat*<br><br><b>"Crystal Storm":</b><br>Penultimate book of the Falling Kingdoms series<br><br><i>? best of 2020</i><br><br>Yet another unexpected turn!<br>another change of plans!<br>Change of sides!<br><br>the Plot was exciting, mind-blowing! reserved its biggest blow for the last though! I still can't breathe! &amp; to be fair, every part had a blow itself, by all those reunions &amp; revelations &amp; attacks!<br><br><br><u>
  <b>Characters</b>
</u><br><br>Magnus: No need to say he is AWESOME! strong (won't give in without a fight), sarcastic, strategist, fearless, caring, protective, vulnerable, a total idiot, &amp; a clueless idiot at some points! he disliked anything but black clothes (my brooding bby!) he knows he's not perfect &amp; he admits he made mistakes. his character development since book one is great!<br><br>Jonas: haha! he is another awesome character, funny, rebel, sassy, hothead, caring &amp; again, another clueless idiot at some points!<br><br>Nic: my feeling toward him had its ups &amp; downs, for now; funny, cute but also cheeky. in the end of this book, I liked him.<br><br>Felix: sassy, sarcastic, strong hot-head &amp; an idiot!<br><br>Taran: I liked him. rebel, violent, but reasonable.<br><br>Enzo!: such a cute &amp; underrated character!<br><br>Strong female characters:<br>Lucia: at last she matured! (especially after that spoiled anger-blind girl in book 4! though I like that side of her, except that she didn't see the reason &amp; that was when she was acting like a baby!)<br><br>Cleo: She is a strong woman &amp; had rough character developments, but still she is able to make me angry at some points I want to strangle her!<br><br>Amara: I admire Amara, but I didn't totally like her chapters, which was more descriptive than the others. but she is also ruthless &amp; heartless, so I don't know how I feel toward her.<br><br>Nerissa could be my favourite.<br><br><br>I found another ship here! &amp; probably two Frenemies!<br>The romance was beautiful!<br>&amp; complicated!<br>I didn't know how much I loved a well-built, slowly-created Enemies to Lovers trope! (I always thought, how is that even possible!? in this series I saw how that was Possible &amp; it was beautiful! I needed it!)<br><br>I will JUMP into next book right now! BYE!<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1587144407i/29308919.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>feeling evolution toward the SHIP in the series:<br><br><b>"Might be Spoiler if you haven't read book 3 &amp; 4"</b><br><br><br><br>beginning of book 3:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1580491011ra/28880825.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>End of Book 3:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1580535044ra/28883069.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Book 4:<br>Then:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1580491182ra/28880853.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>&amp;<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1585163596ra/29168649.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Now:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1587566165ra/29337649.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>&amp; at last book 5:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1580535044ra/28883070.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1871231911" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1871231911" />
    <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines"><img alt="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466111136p2/30004027.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1871231911?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines">Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780448494166" href="/book/show/33371681-crystal-storm">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1871231911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13408454526844605348">Am I allowed to faint?<br/><blockquote>
  <i>"This is war. And in war, we must do what is necessary to survive."</i>
</blockquote><br/><b>4,5 stars</b><br/><br/><u>Spoilers below</u><br/><br/>Dear people of planet earth, it is the first time that three books of the same series make it to my favourite shelve (Harry Potter isn’t counting here). And the reason is simple: <b>MAGNEO</b>. I just ship them so bad. And I loved the fact that even if they professed their love in the previous instalment, <b>being in a couple wasn’t an easy-cheesy road</b>, they both kept their struggles, greed </span>
  <span id="freeText13408454526844605348" style="display:none">Am I allowed to faint?<br><blockquote>
  <i>"This is war. And in war, we must do what is necessary to survive."</i>
</blockquote><br><b>4,5 stars</b><br><br><u>Spoilers below</u><br><br>Dear people of planet earth, it is the first time that three books of the same series make it to my favourite shelve (Harry Potter isn’t counting here). And the reason is simple: <b>MAGNEO</b>. I just ship them so bad. And I loved the fact that even if they professed their love in the previous instalment, <b>being in a couple wasn’t an easy-cheesy road</b>, they both kept their struggles, greed and ambition. Their scenes were so catchy, I couldn’t put the book down. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483316947i/21600607._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>It went from butterfly in my stomach to the nauseating sickness</b>. Magnus was more open as he expressed his feelings more, owned up to them even, whereas Cleo kept some distance, especially because she cares about what others may think (and by other I mean Nic). She has to keep a mask and she does it too well for my taste. And even if she stays a master of deception, I still want them both together, because <b>she can make Magnus happy, and I just need him smiling</b>, please, it would be the most beautiful gift ever. <br><br>Below, with a full-page quote, you can witness both the sexual tension and the desire that drives them, but also my poor baby’s feeling hurting him:<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <blockquote>Magnus took a step closer to her; she took a step backwards: the same dance they engaged in from time to time. They kept it up until he backed her into a corner, and she looked up at him defiantly.<br><br><i>“Perhaps you’d rather share a room with the rebel than with me,” he said, twisting a lock of her hair around his finger. “Then again, he’d probably prefer a house in the trees made of sticks and mud.”</i><br><br>Cleo scoffed. <i>“This is what you choose to focus on right now?” <br><br>“Yes. Because if I focus on Agallon, I can stop focusing on you and how badly I want to take you to my bed.” </i><br><br>All she could do was let out a brief, breathy gasp before his lips were on hers, his hands gripping her waist and pulling her against him. And she kissed him back without reservation.<br><br>His hands slid down her sides to her waist, around to the small of her back, and over the curve of her bottom. Frustrated with the necessity to lean over to fully kiss her, he gripped the backs of her thighs and lifted her up into his arms so that her back pressed up against the wall.<br><br>Surely, she would stop him now.<br><br>And yet she didn’t. In fact, she’d begun to frantically pull at the ties of his shirt, her mouth not leaving his for an instant.<br><br><i>“I want you,” </i> he whispered against her lips. <i>“I want you so much I may die from it.”<br><br>“Yes . . .”</i> Her breath was so sweet, so warm. <i>“I want you too.” </i><br><br>When he kissed her next, all rational thought about the curse vanished from his mind. There was nothing except the maddening, blinding need to touch her, to taste her . . .<br><br>At least, not until he heard the footsteps approaching from behind him.<br><br>It was then that Magnus sensed that they were no longer alone.<br><br>Slowly lowering the princess back to the ground, Magnus forced himself to pull away from her and, shoulders tense, look upon their intruder.<br><br>Despite his intimidating stature and impressive muscle, Felix Gaebras looked positively sheepish.<br><br><i>“Um . . . sorry to interrupt? I was . . . uh . . . just moving through.”</i> But he remained still where he stood, then raised his chin. <i>“Pardon me for saying, your highness,”</i> he said, looking at Magnus, <i>“but you might want to be more discreet with the princess from now on.”<br><br>“Is that so?”</i> Magnus hissed.<br><br>Felix nodded. <i>“Nic has happily convinced everyone that you hate Magnus, princess. And that . . . didn’t look like an act of hate to me. He’s going to go out of his mind over this.”</i><br><br>Cleo stepped away from Magnus, her fingers pressed to her lips and her cheeks bright red.<br><br><i>“Please, Felix,”</i> she said, almost desperately. <i>“Promise me that you won’t tell Nic about this. Not ever.”</i><br><br>Felix bowed. <i>“Don’t worry, princess. I won’t breathe a word.”<br><br>“Thank you.”</i><br><br>Magnus hid his grimace. Something about how she said it, how relieved she sounded that it had only been Felix who’d witnessed them together and not someone whose opinion she valued more, pained him deeply.</blockquote>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17342701.Frozen_Tides__Falling_Kingdoms___4_" title="Frozen Tides (Falling Kingdoms, #4) by Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Frozen Tides</a> stays my absolute favourite but this book was still amazing. I think this is the first book where I can bear most of the side characters. They accepted their fate as side characters, they were here to help fulfil the main quest without trying to steal the spotlight from the one we love. <b>Surprisingly, Jonas became interesting and at last useful. He was more levelheaded and rational;</b> he tried to think before acting, not driven by bitterness or grudge. His storyline evolved giving him a key role.<br><br>To me, Lucia was useless, I really would prefer a book without her point-of-view, but at least, someone gave her some sense back. She was boring but at least she was redeeming herself. However, <b>I liked how she and Jonas met and had to put their hard feelings aside to collaborate for the greater good.</b> Felix was good but we didn’t get his POV, and I’m like Taran who? Please, tell me what is the purpose of this character?<br><br>Last but not least, we got Amara. And I want to give her the award of the <b>most annoying and boring POV ever made</b>. At first, I could sympathize with her loneliness and her need to belong and be a part of something bigger, but now I just hated her. I was just like, okay, we get it, you want to be the empress of the world, man must kneel before you, you are oh-so-ruthless. Please, change the record now, will you?<br><blockquote>
  <i>“What do you care of Magnus’s fate, Cleo?” Amara asked, her voice holding a tremor that Cleo had never heard before. “I thought you hated him.”<br><br>“You’re wrong, I don’t hate him,” Cleo managed softly. Then stronger: “I love him. I love Magnus with all my heart. And I swear, if he’s... dead... if I’ve lost both Nic and Magnus today...” Her voice broke as she raised her gaze, seeing that the others now watched her with fear in their eyes. The bottomless sensation of cool, powerful water magic flowed just beneath the surface of her skin, as if waiting to be unleashed. <b>“I don’t think this world will survive my grief.”</b></i>
</blockquote><br>Now I’m so broken to wait for almost a year with that cliffhanger. Please <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5295120.Morgan_Rhodes" title="Morgan Rhodes" rel="nofollow noopener">Morgan Rhodes</a>, take care of Magneo for me. <b>I couldn’t survive if something happened to them</b>. And also, some piece of advice, you can make a book with only those two POV, I think most of the fandom will thank you <i>wink wink ;)</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13408454526844605348" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1369132173" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1796895936347861132">Man, each book in this series is better than the last one. Crystal Storm is no exception. <br/><br/>The story took a bit for me to get captivated, but that's usually the case with these books. There are so many characters and so many POVs, it always takes some time to get situated. However, once I was, it was amazing. <br/><br/>Lots of things I didn't see coming, alliances, backstabbing, kissing, and pretty much anything else you can think of. Oh, and one hell of an ending. I don't know how I'll survive the wait. <br/><br/>*</span>
  <span id="freeText1796895936347861132" style="display:none">Man, each book in this series is better than the last one. Crystal Storm is no exception. <br /><br />The story took a bit for me to get captivated, but that's usually the case with these books. There are so many characters and so many POVs, it always takes some time to get situated. However, once I was, it was amazing. <br /><br />Lots of things I didn't see coming, alliances, backstabbing, kissing, and pretty much anything else you can think of. Oh, and one hell of an ending. I don't know how I'll survive the wait. <br /><br />**Huge thanks to Razorbill for sending me a finished copy** </span>

<div id="review_1498202545" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1498202545" />
    <a title="Candace Robinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33995641-candace-robinson"><img alt="Candace Robinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1530157383p2/33995641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1498202545?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace Robinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace Robinson" href="/user/show/33995641-candace-robinson">Candace Robinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1498202545" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13619125081122343795">Seriously, I have to wait a whole year???? I just CAN'TTTTTTTTTTTTT! Magnus steals the show here as he always does, and I love every single thing that comes out of his mouth! Of course there had to me drama between Magnus and Cleo, I really hate Nic for some reason, Amara is the most annoying character in this whole series, I actually am starting to really like Lucia, and can Jonas and Lucia just get together already??? Pleaseeeeeeeeeeeeee!<br/><br/>Kyan is still crazy, even without a form! There are a lo</span>
  <span id="freeText13619125081122343795" style="display:none">Seriously, I have to wait a whole year???? I just CAN'TTTTTTTTTTTTT! Magnus steals the show here as he always does, and I love every single thing that comes out of his mouth! Of course there had to me drama between Magnus and Cleo, I really hate Nic for some reason, Amara is the most annoying character in this whole series, I actually am starting to really like Lucia, and can Jonas and Lucia just get together already??? Pleaseeeeeeeeeeeeee!<br /><br />Kyan is still crazy, even without a form! There are a lot of interesting things that happen in this book especially towards the end. This series is just so addicting! <div id="review_1841557464" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1841557464" />
    <a title="ambsreads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads"><img alt="ambsreads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508924675p2/30813900.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1841557464?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=magic">magic</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1841557464" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3980084590759802473"><b>WARNING</b>: This review is incredibly scattered much like my thoughts and feelings for this series. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“When the storm comes, all will be revealed.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>For those who want to avoid my low-key spoilers which I may accidentally not mark: <b>read this series for death, death and more death.</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486329795ra/21904719.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I almost wanted to make a drinking game of how many deaths are in this series. The only problem is I would be in the hospital by half of book one. <br/><br/>What's the worst cliffhanger you've ever read? Hold, and think about it fo</span>
  <span id="freeText3980084590759802473" style="display:none"><b>WARNING</b>: This review is incredibly scattered much like my thoughts and feelings for this series. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“When the storm comes, all will be revealed.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>For those who want to avoid my low-key spoilers which I may accidentally not mark: <b>read this series for death, death and more death.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486329795ra/21904719.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I almost wanted to make a drinking game of how many deaths are in this series. The only problem is I would be in the hospital by half of book one. <br><br>What's the worst cliffhanger you've ever read? Hold, and think about it for a minute. If you cried for days and stressed over it, the <i>Falling Kingdoms</i> series is for you. <i>Especially</i>, <i>Crystal Storm</i>. This book has left me, for lack of better word, <b>shook</b>. So much so that two days later I am still unable to truly write what I feel about this book. <br><br>I can't say much about the plot since this is the <b>fifth</b> book in the series and I want to keep this review as spoiler-free as I possibly can. However, if you read this series, and are of the legal age in your country, make sure to have an alcoholic beverage close by because <b>damn</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486330935ra/21904882.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When it comes to characters we have four leads, with the POV switching between them all and other characters who are introduced. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1486330936i/21904883._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucia, Magnus, Cleo, and Jonas are the main characters, the ones who we have seen since the first book. They are not the same characters as they were then, though. The character development that Morgan Rhodes writes is absolutely <b>amazing</b>. I can't get over the subtle growth to bring all four characters into their power and kickass, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[AKA that scene where Cleo killed a bunch of people with just an <i>arrow</i>, sans bow <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I mean, I hate characters I once loved and I love characters I once hated. That's talent. <br><br>It's not even just the characters that make this story. It is just that so many events happen over the course of such a short book that it is <i>crazy</i>. I honestly can't believe I now have to wait <b>ten</b> months for the next book. Especially with this ending. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486331330ra/21904904.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On another note, can we appreciate the fact Morgan acknowledges Ian Somerhalder as her "future husband" like my TVD heart is screaming.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1470186210" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1470186210" />
    <a title="Julie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32276968-julie"><img alt="Julie" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1470186210?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julie" href="/user/show/32276968-julie">Julie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1470186210" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9465700178935211127"><b>Satisfied but disappointed.</b><br/><br/>Confusing, eh? This book was good; it hit all the right points (Magneo scenes <3), but at the same time I thought the book was very poorly planned out because some of the scenes did not make sense or seemed very contrived. It was actually very slow to pick up in the beginning since most of the characters were confined to exchanging barbs in an action-less environment. <br/><br/><b>SPOILERS Warning.</b><br/><br/><u>The Good. </u><br/><br/><b>Magnus.</b> What did you expect? He was as sassy and sarcastic as ever. He didn</span>
  <span id="freeText9465700178935211127" style="display:none"><b>Satisfied but disappointed.</b><br><br>Confusing, eh? This book was good; it hit all the right points (Magneo scenes &lt;3), but at the same time I thought the book was very poorly planned out because some of the scenes did not make sense or seemed very contrived. It was actually very slow to pick up in the beginning since most of the characters were confined to exchanging barbs in an action-less environment. <br><br><b>SPOILERS Warning.</b><br><br><u>The Good. </u><br><br><b>Magnus.</b> What did you expect? He was as sassy and sarcastic as ever. He didn't need killing and fighting to shine. He's a bright star that carried me through the first 50% of the book. His scenes with Cleo were especially cute, especially the haircombing scene and sketch-book note. I thought his concern about Cleo's safety was endearing, but it was pretty obviously a lie/trap so there you go, more forced angst. -eye roll- Otherwise, no complaints on his end. <br><br><b>Cleo. </b> I'm so conflicted. I loved her scenes with Magnus, but I didn't understand the whole need to keep bringing up the whole "I held a part of heart back despite Magnus being a 101% sweetheart." It didn't help that I hated Nic with my entire being, so for her to constantly put Nic's feelings above Magnus's was very annoying. Taran-induced angst to Magneo was actually very minimal compared to what Nic put the couple through. So fuck you very much Nic, you little weasel. <br><br><b>Lucia. </b> Again. Conflicted. I thought her character development was good, but a bit dramatic. Like she literally did a 180 on her personality, going from a bloodthirsty, I-give-no-shits bitch to an apologetic people pleaser. But hey, I guess pregnancy does that to you. I did love the fact that she acknowledged that as fucked up as Gaius was, he was a great father to her. Much better father to her than he ever was to Magnus, so her concern for his well-being, however misguided, was justified. <br><br><b>Jonas.</b> Thank fuck for his development. He was literally grating on my nerves for the past 3 and a half books. I honestly had no idea how he even made it so far into the series when everyone else was dropping like flies. He was a lot more mature and knew that you had to make compromises, no matter how much you hated the other person. He was honestly SO MUCH better than Nic when it came to dealing Magnus, considering he probably had a more valid reason at hating Magnus than Nic ever did. However, I felt the reasoning behind his "magic" was forced and the only reason he even had it was so that he could be comparable to Lucia. I did think Lucia and him made a good pair. No matter where they end up - frienemies, comrades, lovers, whatever, they were good for each other, especially considering how fucked up they were before in the series.<br><br>So overall, the four mains were very well done. <br><br> <u>The Bad.</u><br>I'm going to keep this short because I could rant for days about certain individuals....-cough- NIC -cough- but I don't want to put in the time or effort into him. <br><br><b>Nic.</b> .....There is so much that I need to say, yet so little time. He made Magneo 10x more frustrating than it had to be, always instigating Taran to kill Magnus because he's too much of a coward himself to do it. Basically Nic was a huge coward, and in doing so, made Cleo a coward too. He hated Magnus, but wasn't willing to do anything about it himself because he knew he had no chance. Instead, he kept egging everyone else stronger than him to hate Magnus AND kept making passive-aggressive comments about him. He seemed to hate Magnus more than Gaius himself, the dude who actually killed his sister, for the sole fact that Magnus was "stealing away" Cleo... <br><br>And don't even get me started on his romance with Ashur... Welp, that trajectory felt like a plane crash... It was intriguing in the beginning of the series, but now it was just pathetic and embodied the "love is blind" cliché. Seriously, Ashur was fishy as fuck and EVERYONE (not just Magnus) was telling Nic that he needed to do something about it and get to the bottom of it. Yet, Nic basically followed Ashur around like a love-sick puppy, salivating for attention. He didn't provide ANY intel on Ashur despite him just disappearing one day. Instead, Nic narrow-mindedly blamed Magnus for everything while choosing to protect Ashur despite the fact that Ashur was the guy everyone believed had stolen the Kindred.<br><br><b>Ashur.</b> The phoenix. 'Nuff said. <br>I don't think any character made me feel as strongly of "I can't" more than Ashur did when he waltzed up to Amara and gave her a "chance to surrender" despite knowing she had the upper hand. Like.....you don't bargain from that position unless you want to die. <br><br><b>Gaius. </b> I'm conflicted on his character development. Yeah, it was nice that he stopped trying to kill his son and destroy the world, but I do not understand why he suddenly wanted to act like a father-figure to Magnus right after trying to kill him. He was genuinely concerned about Magnus's future... And all that is going on in my mind is "Dude, you tried to skewer him 1 week ago, you have absolutely no right to make decisions on Magnus's behalf for the betterment of his future."<br><br><b>Amara. </b> I don't know if I hate her because she's the "villain" of the story or she was just goddamn annoying. Yeah, she was kind of badass when she stood up to her sexist guards, but she was such a terrible ruler, and that had nothing to do with the fact that she was a girl. She felt like she was lost most of the time, constantly needing guidance from Kyan on what to do next, and always blaming her lack of power/Kindred as the reason for her poor leadership... She didn't really do anything for the people but sit on her pretty throne and give speeches to appease the public...so basically Gaius 2.0.<br><br><b>Plot holes. </b> I felt like there were a lot of plot holes if you were to look at the series as a whole. Off the top of my head, I still don't know what the Blood Road was meant for, yet it was such a big deal when Gaius first took over.<br><br>There is probably a lot more to say but I finished this book 2 weeks ago, so I barely remember much. If I ever re-read it, I will probably catch a lot more and update this review. <br><br>-----------------------<br>I have to wait a <b>YEAR </b> before I get to read more Magnus and Cleo? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451975246ra/17627248.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9465700178935211127" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('APfQag2ZCa+DwUgd5ZhbMhE0ee5nNwTShK3wVmhw/2gyDj9VcuPGMSN5YdSEG/tBukHe5Hz+SrOVhVBmRx0wyg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RhaKfHSzc91IGQlOQXeL4m2SSXgMrn41PAQHPIRc8tl072VDC8m8Q+ihIIcg9CuRxufuchdnMFQtLKcMqzE9ew==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer17295462695143450439">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet vor</span>
  <span id="freeText17295462695143450439" style="display:none">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet voracious reader of all kinds of books. Under another pen name, she’s a national bestselling author of many paranormal novels. Falling Kingdoms is her first high fantasy. </span>
